! A good deal of these variants belong to the same
! CC as the headwords, because they only slightly
! change, e.g. ainbhiosán->ainbhiosachán.
! If the gender changes, a direct mapping is often possible,
! e.g. adhaltranas (Nm1-SINGULAR) -> adhaltraíocht (Nf3-SINGULAR).
! Sometimes, however, the assignment of the CC is just a 'best guess' 
! and may need to be revised.
! CW 28/08/08
